  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_bf5b308e-b0a2-43bb-ad78-128b13efd8fc'
      });

          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {

              return;

            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});

<a href="/questions/1731158-pls-can-anyone-recommend-a-writer-like">Pls can anyone recommend a writer like Joey W. Hill? I&#39;ve searched everywhere and she&#39;s one of the few writing proper BDSM. A balanced combination of intensity and heart. Adult. No first person books pls. A good alpha/dominant/femdom. Not too much angst/slow burn. And well written sex scenes! I welcome uncomfortable scenes.</a>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Like Joey W. Hill author Tymber Dalton walks the talk. Her stories aren't paranormal but more like real life. Tymber is staff at a BDSM dungeon in Tam<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Like Joey W. Hill author Tymber Dalton walks the talk. Her stories aren't paranormal but more like real life. Tymber is staff at a BDSM dungeon in Tampa and writes what she knows. My very favorite book of hers, and her most popular is The Reluctant Dom. It's the fourth book in her Suncoast Society series. It's a big tearjerker. Tymber is incredibly prolific and currently has 97 books in that series. This is solely how she makes a living. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer512484620" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7403810831632530954"><b>6/2020<br/><br/>It's been SIX YEARS since I last read this????</b><br/><br/>Where the hell does the time go?<br/><br/>I actually thought this one got a little long-winded but the fact that I've read it this many times means I'm not coming off those stars.<br/><br/>Ever.<br/><br/>•••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br/><br/>5/14-I still love it. This triad has become a comfort read for me.<br/><br/><b>Can I give more than 5 stars????</b> <br/><br/>Gideon is a notorious vampire hunter who also happens to be Jacob’s brother-Jacob who’s married </span>
  <span id="freeText7403810831632530954" style="display:none"><b>6/2020<br /><br />It's been SIX YEARS since I last read this????</b><br /><br />Where the hell does the time go?<br /><br />I actually thought this one got a little long-winded but the fact that I've read it this many times means I'm not coming off those stars.<br /><br />Ever.<br /><br />•••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br /><br />5/14-I still love it. This triad has become a comfort read for me.<br /><br /><b>Can I give more than 5 stars????</b> <br /><br />Gideon is a notorious vampire hunter who also happens to be Jacob’s brother-Jacob who’s married to Lyssa (Vampire Queen of the Far East Clan). Gideon is also a lost, lonely and tortured soul until one fateful night he walks into Anwyn’s BDSM club looking for something but not quite sure what. Anwyn is <i>the</i> formidable Mistress of Club Atlantis who notices Gideon right away but allows him to basically mow through 3 other Mistresses of the club before she intervenes. Gideon responds to her immediately but the wrinkle is Anwyn is involved with Daegan-vampire assassin extraordinaire. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Poor Gideon… can’t seem to escape the vamps-kind of ironic that the fate of a vampire hunter is with not one but two vampires. Bet he didn’t see that coming! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Throughout the reading of this I kept having old adages run through my mind like: ‘still waters run deep’ or ‘don’t judge a book by its cover’ as Gideon is a man of few words but there are so many emotions that lie just beneath the surface. He is the master of deflection via humor as well as denial. He’s such a well constructed not to mention complex character it’s hard not to love him. He can break your heart and have you laughing within the span of a few minutes. <br /><br />Daegan at this point is mostly an enigma. We don’t get much info on him other than he and Anwyn have a relationship which involves her submitting to him. Only him. Anwyn is tough as nails which is part of the reason she's never become Daegan's servant. She’s also got a 747 worth of baggage and has to relying on both Daegan and Gideon to help her get through her transition. She's exceptional at compartmentalizing her issues and focusing on the task at hand ordinarily, but her transition is challenging and wrests her control. <br /><br />I have to be honest I’ve been clamoring to get to Gideon’s story since he was introduced. Don’t get me wrong I enjoyed the other books in the series but these two were spectacular. In fact, I got so engrossed that I didn’t even review this one prior to starting and finishing <i>Vampire Trinity</i>. But, I will try not to mix the reviews. This one mainly focuses on the development of Gideon and Anwyn’s relationship, coaxing Gideon to admit the possibility of having feelings for Daegan as well. I will say if I’d had had to wait a year to read the conclusion to this I probably would’ve had to rock myself to sleep for many MANY nights. Thankfully, that was not the case.</span>

<div id="review_317444073" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/317444073" />
    <a title="Ilhem" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8110617-ilhem"><img alt="Ilhem" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1362861103p2/8110617.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/317444073?book_show_action=true">Apr 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ilhem" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ilhem" href="/user/show/8110617-ilhem">Ilhem</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8110617-ilhem?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8110617-ilhem?shelf=prn">prn</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8110617-ilhem?shelf=bdsm">bdsm</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer317444073" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11761819319486246734">I thought that Joey W. Hill did an honourable job with this book, turning worn-out themes into a rather smart and good story.<br/><br/>Gideon is a vampire hunter, overwhelmed by guilt and grief since the woman he loved was killed by a vampire. Pure tortured Alpha male with a knight-in-shining-armour complex and I can see you rolling your eyes!<br/>Daegan is a vampire, tall, dark and broody (duh), powerful and dominant.<br/>Anwyn is a Dominatrix, owner of a BDSM club and already involved in a relationship with the a</span>
  <span id="freeText11761819319486246734" style="display:none">I thought that Joey W. Hill did an honourable job with this book, turning worn-out themes into a rather smart and good story.<br /><br />Gideon is a vampire hunter, overwhelmed by guilt and grief since the woman he loved was killed by a vampire. Pure tortured Alpha male with a knight-in-shining-armour complex and I can see you rolling your eyes!<br />Daegan is a vampire, tall, dark and broody (duh), powerful and dominant.<br />Anwyn is a Dominatrix, owner of a BDSM club and already involved in a relationship with the above mentioned vampire when she meets Gideon in her club. I got interested in this story because I liked her and this quote sums up her character pretty well : <b>
  <i>(…)”her lips had curved, a tear caught on that tremulous but brave upward turn.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Indeed, not long after the beginning, Anwyn is savagely attacked, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[raped, very badly hurt and turned into a vampire <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, discovered bleeding in an alley by her two Alpha males.<br />My interest in the story persisted because Gideon and Daegan don’t go strolling in the setting sun on an avenging rampage to soothe their <b>
  <i>”male rage, so helpless in a situation like this, a desperate need to give her back what had been destroyed”</i>
</b><br />Instead, it is a closed door story where they become her jailers as well as her care takers while she’s struggling to come to terms with what happened and her new self, each man exploring his relationship with her.<br /><b>
  <i>”What she needed was a cocoon of generous, passive emotion to rock in, like a quiet ocean. In that quiet, maybe she could coax her hiding soul from the dark shadows into which it had fled”</i>
</b><br /><br />My complaint is that it was too long and therefore didn’t avoid a few reefs.<br />Confined places are fine for enhanced emotions, deep introspection and character growth but the story and the characters start to choke on their own breath after too long. <br />The author often kept turning over the same inner turmoil and those moments were useless and irritating. They disconnected me from the characters and pulled me out of the story.<br />At last, I dislike it when an author explains me the pros and cons and whys of the characters’ actions.<br /><br />To conclude. <br />Despite a few reserves, I liked <i>Vampire Mistress</i> and will read the follow-on “<i>Vampire Trinity</i><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11761819319486246734" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_97460428" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/97460428" />
    <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner"><img alt="Mandi Schreiner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368979996p2/2704703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/97460428?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mandi Schreiner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mandi Schreiner" href="/user/show/2704703-mandi-schreiner">Mandi Schreiner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer97460428" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12678802855609618304"><strong>Why I read: </strong>Received for review from the publisher.<br/><strong>
  <br/>
</strong><br/><strong>Favorite Quote:</strong> “<em>Anwyn</em>.” Daegan caught her shoulders. <br/>The vampire’s command resonated through the bathroom, and possibly the entire lower level. Gideon knew generals – not to mention high school teachers – who would give a left nut to freeze motion and rivet attention as Daegan did with two syllables. Who the hell was this guy?<br/><strong>
  <br/>
</strong><br/><strong>Favorite Naughty Quote:</strong> Daegan set aside the lubricant, his hand still working himself. That glistening tumescen</span>
  <span id="freeText12678802855609618304" style="display:none"><strong>Why I read: </strong>Received for review from the publisher.<br><strong>
  <br>
</strong><br><strong>Favorite Quote:</strong> “<em>Anwyn</em>.” Daegan caught her shoulders. <br>The vampire’s command resonated through the bathroom, and possibly the entire lower level. Gideon knew generals – not to mention high school teachers – who would give a left nut to freeze motion and rivet attention as Daegan did with two syllables. Who the hell was this guy?<br><strong>
  <br>
</strong><br><strong>Favorite Naughty Quote:</strong> Daegan set aside the lubricant, his hand still working himself. That glistening tumescent organ slid through his clenched long fingers like a living beast.<br><br>Vampire hunter, Gideon Green is a tortured soul. He spends his days hunting vampires that have killed innocents, all the while dealing with his brother Jacob who was recently turned into a vampire. Gideon is yearning for something – anything to turn his soul from the blackness that is enveloping it.  He ends up at BDSM Nightclub Atlantis owned by Anwyn – a Domme herself. She knows Gideon is more violent and aggressive than the normal men she lets into the club, but she sees something in him – something not at all unfamiliar to her. <br><br>Gideon refuses the three mistresses Anwyn sends in, sending him over the edge in pure rage. But when Anwyn herself walks in, and demands him to become submissive – something shifts in Gideon. Gideon is not a submissive, but he is searching for loyalty, to be used for service. All parts of his body want to rebel, but he hangs onto a thread of hope that Anwyn can strip him down to his base self.<br><blockquote>
<br>Anwyn felt his yearning, a gas fire that threatened to consume. It was too similar to what she knew and remembered, and she felt oddly stripped as she looked into his face and saw how lost he truly was, this feral creature who’d come to her door, not sure if he wanted to bed for a bowl of scraps or break in and take whatever he wanted.</blockquote><br>Anwyn feels something special about Gideon, something she has only felt for one other person – Daegan Rei. Daegan is a very old, very powerful vampire whom has protected and shared a relationship with Anwyn for years. Anwyn has refused to become Daegan’s servant, refusing those three marks it takes. Daegan doesn’t accept no easily, and for him to accept Anwyn to remain human shows he cares for her deeply. Daegan notices the spark in Anwyn’s eye when she looks at Gideon and knows this man is something different.<br><br>When Anwyn gets brutally attacked later that night in an alley by rogue vampires, she gets thrust into the world she was trying to avoid. All of Gideon’s instincts scream at him that this is wrong, but his heart knows he can’t harm Anwyn. To keep her alive, he is going to have to face his biggest fears and learn to trust and live with those he has hunted and hated.<br><br>Oh Joey W. Hill, where have you been all my life? Writing tons of books I’ve never read? *cry* <strong>
  <em>Vampire Mistress</em>
</strong> is the first book I have read by Joey W. Hill and I was blown away. I absolutely loved this book. Usually erotic paranormal ménage makes me run and hide. But, I received this in the mail, and many people have recommended this author to me so I dove in. I honestly think this is the first ménage book that 100% works for me. The dynamics of the three people in this relationship are amazing. There is Anwyn, the very dominant female who has a complicated relationship with a very dominant vampire. She refuses to submit herself to become his servant and he refuses to submit his true feelings that he loves her. They both care deeply for each other, but their relationship is on a static hold.<br><br>Then Gideon enters the picture – the brutal, tortured Gideon who will lay down his life to protect a female, especially Anwyn, who he has a life altering connection to. But he will also fight to the death against vampires that he has an absolute hatred for. He has a very cocky attitude with a sarcastic mouth that made me smile many times throughout this book. When Anwyn is turned – for him to put aside his presumptions, for him to be able to work and trust Daegan, it is really a remarkable journey Joey W. Will takes him on. These two fierce men are forced to work together to save the woman they love, and in doing so, they start breaking down the walls that each have held up their whole lives.<br><br>Anwyn pushes the sexual boundaries in this book, and for me, it is the perfect mix. The way she strips Gideon down, bares his soul – puts him into sexual situations with Daegan, is beautifully done. Joey W. Hill takes these characters just far enough. She gives us very erotic sex, and just a hint of Daegan and Gideon together, as they please Anwyn to make their scenes together extremely erotic. Like I said, I am not huge into erotic ménage – but I became so emotionally invested in these three characters, that I could not imagine it working out any other way.<br><br>We also see the journey of Anwyn physically and mentally changing into a vampire and it is not pretty at all. It is horrifying and raw, and adds another level to this book. The Domme Anwyn now has to give up all control and put her trust into these two men.<br><br>Their story is not done yet though. Coming this September is <em>
  <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Vampire-Trinity-Queen-Joey-Hill/dp/0425236706?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=smeboo-20&amp;link_code=btl&amp;camp=213689&amp;creative=392969" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Vampire Trinity</a>
  <img alt="" height="1" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333775i/693457.gif" width="1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</em> which will conclude this trio’s story and I am on pins and needles to get my hands on it. I already have the first four books on their way to me and can’t wait to read more of Joey W. Hill’s work. <strong>
  <em>Vampire Mistress</em>
</strong> will definitely make my favorite list this year. The erotic nature may not work for everyone, and I can’t pinpoint exactly why this book affected me so much.  However, it is a book I very much recommend.<br><strong>
  <br>
</strong><br><strong>Rating: 4.5/5</strong><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12678802855609618304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_271015278" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/271015278?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.A." class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.A." href="/user/show/4720883-s-a">S.A.</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer271015278" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17909840221130035627">Sorry, this book suffers from the Laurell K. Hamilton school of long, verbose sex scenes. It suffers from the cliche "oooo, two alpha males and oh hell NO I AM NOT GAY but ooo, I like it when another male touches me" thang. Maybe that's not a thang, but I find it fairly hilarious. <br/><br/>There was one line, damn, I wished I had placed a marker at the page, which had me rolling on the floor. Wait, I found it. "She'd also seen two situations where two men loved, but never thought of themselves as gay. Sh</span>
  <span id="freeText17909840221130035627" style="display:none">Sorry, this book suffers from the Laurell K. Hamilton school of long, verbose sex scenes. It suffers from the cliche "oooo, two alpha males and oh hell NO I AM NOT GAY but ooo, I like it when another male touches me" thang. Maybe that's not a thang, but I find it fairly hilarious. <br /><br />There was one line, damn, I wished I had placed a marker at the page, which had me rolling on the floor. Wait, I found it. "She'd also seen two situations where two men loved, but never thought of themselves as gay. She liked that. Love shouldn't be stuck in a box with a label."<br /><br />What the milk and cookies? Oh yes, heaven forbid that any of the brooding, cocky alpha males regard themselves as gay. Noooo, that would spoil things for everyone! That did me in.<br /><br />The dialogue also did me in, with all the tough alpha guy "witty" bon mots and retorts. If I hung out with these two, I'd walk away from them.<br /><br />Or tell them to get a room and fuck already.<br /><br />The shame was I really appreciated the female character. She saved the book.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18190961524046650215">4.30am - the time I finished this book this morning after intending only to read a couple of chapters.<br/>All three characters in this story have incredibly complex histories. Opposing yet complimentary, attitudes/views so set yet evolving. The three of them thrown together and all trying to discover who they are as a group and also as individuals.<br/>This is a 3-way romance, brutal in content given the inciting event that throws the characters together but I like the hints that their trinity is going t</span>
  <span id="freeText18190961524046650215" style="display:none">4.30am - the time I finished this book this morning after intending only to read a couple of chapters.<br />All three characters in this story have incredibly complex histories. Opposing yet complimentary, attitudes/views so set yet evolving. The three of them thrown together and all trying to discover who they are as a group and also as individuals.<br />This is a 3-way romance, brutal in content given the inciting event that throws the characters together but I like the hints that their trinity is going to save/give each of them their heart's desire.<br />While the story remains "structured" by the vampire world, I really like how it focuses almost entirely on the three characters melding, with Anwyn's transformation the central driving plot, with only a touch of the external forces/politics (I expect that to play a much greater part in the next book).<br />Daegan Rei has me intrigued, can't wait to find out more about his past in Vampire Trinity (the next book in the series). Loved Gideon Green and his gradual evolution from vampire hunter to vampire servant. Anwyn - wow, what incredible endurance and strength.<br />Vampire Trinity is already beside me and I expect I'll be reading it all today. :-)</span>

<div id="review_121844911" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/121844911" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4295616-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1531866745p2/4295616.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/121844911?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/4295616-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer121844911" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer386805291243457069">I love the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/44111-vampire-queen' rel='nofollow noopener'>Vampire Queen series</a> and I'm OCD when it comes to reading a series in order but you could start with <i>Vampire Mistress</i> and you would be ok. There are a few mentions of previous characters in the other books but nothing that will have you lost. <br/><br/>IMO this book has the most emotional tug of war going on between the characters in the series so far. You've got three strong-willed characters who are looking for something that's missing in their lives. <br/><br/>Gideon is a loner and hates vampires so h</span>
  <span id="freeText386805291243457069" style="display:none">I love the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/44111-vampire-queen" rel="nofollow noopener">Vampire Queen series</a> and I'm OCD when it comes to reading a series in order but you could start with <i>Vampire Mistress</i> and you would be ok. There are a few mentions of previous characters in the other books but nothing that will have you lost. <br /><br />IMO this book has the most emotional tug of war going on between the characters in the series so far. You've got three strong-willed characters who are looking for something that's missing in their lives. <br /><br />Gideon is a loner and hates vampires so he has devoted his life to being the best vampire hunter. <br /><br />Anwyn is the beautiful owner and operator of Atlantis, a BDSM club. <br /><br />Deagan is a dark, mysterious and sexy vampire. <br /><br />Gideon finds himself being drawn to Atlantis and after he doesn't find what he is looking for during 1st and 2nd visit; he gets a visit from the beautiful owner. He knows that she is what he has been needing. But when he finds out that she is in some kind of relationship with a vampire, he pulls away from her. <br /><br />The vampire in question is the mysterious Daegan. He and Anwyn have been in a relationship for 5 years. Deagan is the only person Anwyn will submit to, but she can't allow herself to totally submit to Deagan to become his servant. So the two's relationship is on an edge of either failing or becoming what they both need. That's where Gideon comes in. He could be the missing piece to the puzzle they need to make all three happy.<br /><br />The threesome goes through hell together and is trying to make their way back. All three needs to learn how to submit to one another. But with three dominant characters, it won't be easy. <br /><br />They do not get their HEA in <i>Vampire Mistress</i>, their story continues in <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7874158-vampire-trinity" rel="nofollow noopener">Vampire Trinity</a>
</i>. I'm very much looking forward to seeing how they overcome their personal hang-ups and learn to be a part of the harsh vampire world and it rules.<br /><br /><i>Vampire Mistress</i> is not for the fate at heart. It has violence and emotional roller coaster mixed with strong BDSM elements. But if you are looking for a sexy and intense read pick it up today. <br /><br />I recommend starting at the beginning of the series just so you learn the rules of the vampire/servant roles and get a little background on some of the other characters. But like I said if you wanted to start with this one you won't be lost.</span>
  <a data-text-id="386805291243457069" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17064115077996841614">Since I'm reading these past the publishing dates, I know this is a setup book to the next one. I was a little bored at times, which hadn't yet happened to me in the series. I knew Gideon would be a complex character, and if I didn't know that there was a second book following, I would have felt "jipped." I also felt that we needed a bit more family (i.e. Jacob and Lyssa) interaction, even if it was only in the form of phone calls. Lady Lyssa, of course, had a fabulous LOL quip, which each book </span>
  <span id="freeText17064115077996841614" style="display:none">Since I'm reading these past the publishing dates, I know this is a setup book to the next one. I was a little bored at times, which hadn't yet happened to me in the series. I knew Gideon would be a complex character, and if I didn't know that there was a second book following, I would have felt "jipped." I also felt that we needed a bit more family (i.e. Jacob and Lyssa) interaction, even if it was only in the form of phone calls. Lady Lyssa, of course, had a fabulous LOL quip, which each book seems to deliver. I am glad that Hill always remembers. I may read again after I finish "Trinity," to see if I missed pieces while "bored," as I tend to skim at times.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15749421030152081788">Joey is a new author to me and I chose this book because I saw it promoted on another author's FB page AND it was free! Well if the aim of the exercise was to rope me in, they done me good. I really enjoyed this and the well developed characters this story revolves around, my favourite being Daegan, I could get into some serious trouble with him. To be fair Anwyn and Gideon are also great characters and they all have their own back story which is gradually released throughout this and the second</span>
  <span id="freeText15749421030152081788" style="display:none">Joey is a new author to me and I chose this book because I saw it promoted on another author's FB page AND it was free! Well if the aim of the exercise was to rope me in, they done me good. I really enjoyed this and the well developed characters this story revolves around, my favourite being Daegan, I could get into some serious trouble with him. To be fair Anwyn and Gideon are also great characters and they all have their own back story which is gradually released throughout this and the second book in this tale, Vampire Trinity.<br />The majority of the book is spent within the walls of Club Atlantis, a BDSM club which is Anwyn's business. I'm not going to say too much about the plot and give the story away but fair to say Anwyn has a serious incident which requires her to be confined within the basement of the club and our two heroes make it their goal to help her through this period in her life. Gideon ends up becoming something he should in theory abor (and he does struggle) and probably if I had read the previous books in the series I may have known more about him. Having said all that I felt the author made an expert job of keeping me absorbed whilst staying within these walls.<br />If you like Vampire books with plenty of spice I would definitely recommend this book and it's follow up Vampire Trinity. Although I haven't read previous books in the series it would seem that it is not necessary to enjoy the tale of these three characters, I will however be looking to read them some time soon.</span>

  <span id="freeText13258228312770516638" style="display:none">Well, well, well. I took a break from the Vampire Queen world after binge reading the first four books. In between, I read the Twilight Saga for the first time in nearly ten years (ugh!). Now Joey W. Hill writes about REAL vampires, ones that are badass, realistic, and just plain sexy.<br /><br />I met Gideon back in book number two, "The Mark of the Vampire Queen", and he was the typical vampire hunter with a troubled past. Nothing new. Boring. Blegh. When I learned he had his own book (two, in fact), I was hesitant. My first impression of him was dull. Yeah, the sex scene between him, Jacob, and Lady Lyssa was kinda hot, but only because Lady Lyssa was there. *PSST!* I would loooove to be her servant, hehehe.<br /><br />Anwyn, though, made it all worth it. That woman is just mind blowing. I felt her dominance right from the start. Within two pages she had my attention. She brought out something in Gideon that I was not expecting. Now I love the guy. His smartass attitude is awesome, his baggage is something I connected with, and he just came off the page. I look forward to the next book.<br /><br />But, after a while everything got sluggish, hence the 3 stars. I love Joey's writing, but nothing major happened. Yes, Anwy is brutally raped and forced to become a vampire, but...something was just missing. I wanted to see more of Daegan. The sex scenes rocked, but like I said. Something was amiss. I guess I just wanted more to happen.</span>

<div id="review_1040553168" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1040553168" />
    <a title="Isabel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10916626-isabel"><img alt="Isabel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393678460p2/10916626.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1040553168?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Isabel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Isabel" href="/user/show/10916626-isabel">Isabel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10916626-isabel?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10916626-isabel?shelf=d-s">d-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10916626-isabel?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1040553168" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3386757219178171227">Now is Gideon Green's story.<br/><br/>I disliked this character while reading Lyssa and Jacob's books. I haven't been reading the Vampire Queen series in order, so it was a surprise seeing Gideon from a unhappy and tormented vampire hunter turning into a servant in 'Bound by the Vampire Queen', even more... two vampires' servant!! That picked my curiosity at the time, but as Bound by the Vampire Queen was a bit disappointing, I took a break from the series. It has been now, months later, after reading the</span>
  <span id="freeText3386757219178171227" style="display:none">Now is Gideon Green's story.<br /><br />I disliked this character while reading Lyssa and Jacob's books. I haven't been reading the Vampire Queen series in order, so it was a surprise seeing Gideon from a unhappy and tormented vampire hunter turning into a servant in 'Bound by the Vampire Queen', even more... two vampires' servant!! That picked my curiosity at the time, but as Bound by the Vampire Queen was a bit disappointing, I took a break from the series. It has been now, months later, after reading the Xmas vignettes that I wanted to know how Gideon became a bisexual guy sworn to serve and feed not one but two vampires. <br /><br />Of course, as any drama worthy to be called such in erotica, the story starts with a woman's rape. (you would think that being female vampires impossibly stronger than normal men, you would find doable a dominant male owner of a BDSM club being raped and traumatized by female vampires... but not, still is considered taboo in erotica to make Dominant men victims of stronger females, vampires or else, perhaps authors lack the imagination to describe vampires' vaginas that actually can hurt human penises at the vagina's owner's will...). <br /><br />We follow Gideon taking a short break after his last kill. He needs strong physical interactions that balance his heavy emotional baggage, and for once he doesn't get himself a hooker, but tries something different and seeks it in a BDSM club. He lost his sweetheart at the hands of a vampire years ago, he lost his parents when he was a child, and finally he ‘lost’ his brother when he became a vampire’s servant and later turned a vampire himself. Basically Gideon seems to be the unluckiest man on earth...<br /><br />But then, he is actually found by a woman with a story of lost too (and yes yes yes of course... she also was raped in her childhood), and it seems that for once there is something worth to pursue in his life besides vampires. Then that very woman is attacked and... guess what? gang raped by vampires and turned into one, just Gideon’s luck... So from there Gideon has a first row seat on the transformation from a human to a unstable vampire (just the kind of vampires he hunts and kills), and is interesting to see his evolution, how he deals with the fact of reckless vampires being themselves victims, without losing his identity and his principles as a vampire hunter. He by no means accepts neither justifies the killing of humans by vampires (even the annual kill), and this strong pillar of his beliefs keeps being tested while helping Anwyn in her traumatic and forced transition. <br /><br />Then we have Daegan Rei, a mysterious vampire who is Anwyn’s lover (and her Dominant, because you know... submissive male vampires are science fiction even in a fictional vampire world...), which means Anwyn is a switch, Dominant to male humans, submissive to male vampires. He is nothing less than a vampire hunter himself, commissioned by the Vampire Council to ‘clean’ the vampire world of new made vampires who with their recklessness can expose them to the human world. Daegan has skills and gifts who makes him different from the rest of vampires, lives in the shadows, not subject to the interactions of the vampire society. He is a high rank, a seven hundred years old born vampire, and his mother was a council member, but his name and very existence is only known by the Council. <br /><br />His outcast status together with his occupation, makes of him both a fascinating and frightening creature who inspires as strong loyalties and betrayals. And is this betrayal from some members of the council that caused the attack to Anwyn, for which he feels the only person to blame.<br /><br />The three of them cross their paths after Anwyn’s gang rape and conversion. Daegan and Gideon make a forced truce while looking after Anwyn, finding themselves in the impossible situation of looking after the kind of vampire they both have been killing for most of their lives, and getting to know each other, testing their limits and skills. <br /><br />Gideon reveals more of his personality, besides his tormented dark side. He is daring and challenging, and I love the fact he doesn’t chicken against Daegan, for all the mysterious almightiness that surrounds the vampire assassin and his proven superiority against Gideon. <br />He is rough and caressing, and exposes his human weaknesses which almost get him killed by the unstable and chaotic Anwyn. And yes... he also struggles to resist the inevitable halo of carnality and desire that vampires exhale, even male vampires. We witness his shock at feeling sexually attracted to Daegan. Of course he knows enough about vampires to know they don’t discriminate genders from their sexual interactions, but he always kept vampires at a safe killing distance, the only time he ever fell under that kind of sexual vampire’s spell was when Lyssa took him and his brother in a torrid ménage a trois. <br /><br />With Daegan, he cannot do anything to protect himself from his erotic influence. And having Daegan gained his respect with his fighting skills and arsenal of sophisticated weapons just adds to that involuntary attraction. That for me was the best part, the internal conflict of contradictory feelings and desires towards the male vampire. And Daegan, being Daegan, exercises his subtle and irrevocable flirtation with Gideon, getting him wrapped in his sexual web without even making an open claim. For once, the ‘I-am-not gay-but...’ excuse makes sense, vampires have the power to destroy any human sexual orientation when they seduce.<br /><br />I enjoyed the book, still has the over used ‘alpha male’ label attached to Gideon each time he submits, which seems to be a constant in Joey Hill’s books when defining submissive males (like... you know, he may be submissive but he is very alpha), and the lower rank too (again, is so difficult to show an invincible male assassin born vampire submitting to a female human???), if you have a powerful male, you ‘must’ be dominant, if you are a female (either powerful or weak, dominant or submissive), you ‘must’ have had to be raped. And if you are a male submissive, there will always be a male 120% dominant with the highest status to show that male + submission is a thing for the ‘lower class’. <br /><br />Besides that, I like Gideon's story :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3386757219178171227" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText18274115334993504823" style="display:none">Vampire Mistress is an intense and emotional read.<br /><br />My heart breaks for Gideon. A lost and tortured soul who seeks redemption. He is a vampire hunter. When Gideon visits Club Atlantis he is immediately drawn to Arwyn but is conflicted that Daegan is her Master.<br /><br />Anwyn is the Mistress of Club Atlantis. She's been with Daegan, her Master and a vampire, for a long time but never his servant. Her dominatrix brings men to their knees. She realizes Gideon has a special need. Will she be able to convince him what that need is?<br /><br />Daegan is a vampire executioner. He hides in the shadows. He's in love with Arwyn. He feels Gideon is a threat to them.<br /><br />When Anwyn is attacked Gideon and Daegan must put their differences aside to care for Anwyn whose transition has gone really bad.<br /><br />Can't wait for Vampire Trinity!!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xdoMRYrFnFKEc6LwN9iYsHx1r+fo6P8HB/gsg/ziK72wC16JCAl4NUrEFmy/IHT0EyOLvCUPrqHDzEwFPLsTow==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/jF9U8vxlR/qyG2MEIKbcbNeDiFX9daEjlN2xjTfOA2L4C+fST1xeCR/2RCYenc13AgqepoShyJKZxZA9IYAEw==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText8640854087818184052" style="display:none">"BDSM Romance for the Heart &amp; Soul"<br /><br />Unforgettable alpha males and strong female protagonists are the hallmarks of Joey W. Hill's work in the contemporary and paranormal BDSM romance genres. She has everything from boardroom executives, cops and housemaids to vampires, mermaids, witches and angels. A submissive herself, Hill brings authenticity to her intensely emotional BDSM love stories.<br /><br />With forty award-winning titles and five series available, she also has something for every romance reader wanting the perfect escape read.
